	writefile_3();

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): 3p/minify/src/CSS.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('3p/minify/src/CSS.php') != '410c98087d34ec8cf07ced9044858a437aa170e5') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): 3p/minify/src/CSS.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('3p/minify/src/CSS.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of 3p/minify/src/CSS.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/src/CSS.php') !== '410c98087d34ec8cf07ced9044858a437aa170e5') {
		if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/src/CSS.php') !== '0250eb1917d0eac9e4eebbd55115b4dbdeb1b6f3') {

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('3p/minify/src/CSS.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/src/CSS.php') !== '410c98087d34ec8cf07ced9044858a437aa170e5') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): 3p/minify/src/CSS.php');

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: 3p/minify/src/JS.php');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('3p/minify/src/JS.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): 3p/minify/src/JS.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('3p/minify/src/JS.php') != '15db2ab8ae5d7089d8470989237c9b17d1a95320') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): 3p/minify/src/JS.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('3p/minify/src/JS.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of 3p/minify/src/JS.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/src/JS.php') !== '15db2ab8ae5d7089d8470989237c9b17d1a95320') {
		if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/src/JS.php') !== '81f6e7ac64969b77906ef181cdf5ee59b5f83d25') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: 3p/minify/src/JS.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('3p/minify/src/JS.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('3p/minify/src/JS.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('3p/minify/src/JS.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/src/JS.php') !== '15db2ab8ae5d7089d8470989237c9b17d1a95320') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): 3p/minify/src/JS.php');
		}
	}

if (!is_file('3p/minify/src/Minify.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: 3p/minify/src/Minify.php');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('3p/minify/src/Minify.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): 3p/minify/src/Minify.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('3p/minify/src/Minify.php') != 'bcc2a38ffedaa3a24d4eb36f5082cd9a46cc56d3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): 3p/minify/src/Minify.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('3p/minify/src/Minify.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of 3p/minify/src/Minify.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/src/Minify.php') !== 'bcc2a38ffedaa3a24d4eb36f5082cd9a46cc56d3') {
		if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/src/Minify.php') !== 'de15653997585eb70ed8a37328d15d07611efdae') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: 3p/minify/src/Minify.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('3p/minify/src/Minify.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('3p/minify/src/Minify.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('3p/minify/src/Minify.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('3p/minify/src/Minify.php') !== 'bcc2a38ffedaa3a24d4eb36f5082cd9a46cc56d3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): 3p/minify/src/Minify.php');
		}
	}
}

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/adminPages/050_oobe/oobe.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/adminPages/050_oobe/oobe.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/adminPages/050_oobe/oobe.php') !== '59e4fc7a5fa75549d327582c17b111b93acd5e3c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/adminPages/050_oobe/oobe.php');
		}
	}
}

		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '0c0adad6d08d5dd57d5e2c2ef6c3b8218f5d2ca4') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== 'bcee072f6e1329e55a57f5c1810b42e74d82d547') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_8();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '0c0adad6d08d5dd57d5e2c2ef6c3b8218f5d2ca4') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	writefile_13();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') != 'bdc09fc89e3506d51c15522bb93461538b9e9a7e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== 'bdc09fc89e3506d51c15522bb93461538b9e9a7e') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== '1252b3921763765982dc54e337c9bfa11730648c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_13();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== 'bdc09fc89e3506d51c15522bb93461538b9e9a7e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 440\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 440') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
